                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Horo_Horo_no_Mi" title="Horo Horo no Mi">Horo Horo no Mi</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Hollow-Hollow Fruit</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Hollow</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div>
</div>

</section>
</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible" style="color: #DF3982;">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: #E8E8E8">Devil Fruit</th></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Horo_Horo_no_Mi" title="Horo Horo no Mi">Horo Horo no Mi</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Hollow-Hollow Fruit</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Hollow</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><b>"Ghost Princess" Perona</b><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> is the former <a href="/wiki/Officer" title="Officer">commander</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Wild_Zombies" class="mw-redirect" title="Wild Zombies">Wild Zombies</a> and <a href="/wiki/Surprise_Zombies" class="mw-redirect" title="Surprise Zombies">Surprise Zombies</a> of <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a> prior to its collapse.<sup id="cite_ref-Perona_Intro_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Perona_Intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> She was one of the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Mysterious Four</a><sup id="cite_ref-Enigma_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Enigma-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> and one of the major antagonists of the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Saga" title="Thriller Bark Saga">Thriller Bark Saga</a>.
</p><p>After the defeat of <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>'s army and during the timeskip, she begrudgingly helped<sup id="cite_ref-Treating_Zoro_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Treating_Zoro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> and cooperated with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> while in <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>'s home on <a href="/wiki/Kuraigana_Island" title="Kuraigana Island">Kuraigana Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Preparation_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Preparation-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Perona is a short young woman with big, round black eyes and asymmetrical eyelashes on each of her eyelids bottom that may represent eyeliner, she has long waist-length, light pink hair that she keeps tied into two pigtails with black and white flower hairpins. She wears a red crown with a black cross on her head, as well as red lipstick and a thick layer of black eyeliner. Her white long-sleeved three different black heart shapes shirt was short enough to expose her belly.&#160;She wears a red mini cape with a pink ribbon on front. Her black and white striped tights completely cover her legs, and she wears a mini-skirt and a red and gold belt with a heart belt buckle, as well as red buckled boots. She usually keeps her toes pointing inwards in a pigeon-toed manner and carried around a red parasol shaped like a cute version of a mini devil prior to her battle with <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Perona_Intro_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Perona_Intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a child, Perona carried the same parasol and wore the same crown and hairpins but wore her hair in much thicker pigtails and wore a simple, knee-length red dress with a white wave pattern and dots around its center, as well as smaller red boots. She also carried a ghost doll around on a leash and was accompanied by a bear named <a href="/wiki/Kumae" title="Kumae">Kumae</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Child_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Child-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When first meeting <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a> ten years prior to her encounter with the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, Perona wore the same crown, but the rest of her outfit was not clearly visible, though she seemed to be wearing a similar dress.<sup id="cite_ref-Recruiting_Hogback_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Recruiting_Hogback-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the two-year timeskip, Perona has a more mature look than before, wearing a long black strapless dress with lavender frills, red high heeled boots and a big black top hat with white floral decor. She has a pink bat tattoo on her left bicep and a watch on her left wrist and wears pink nail polish on her fingernails. She still has her signature parasol, and also carries a stuffed animal resembling <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a> with her. Additionally, she now wears her hair in multiple spiral braids on the back of her head.<sup id="cite_ref-Post-Timeskip_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Post-Timeskip-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While reading about the Straw Hats' actions on <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa" title="Dressrosa">Dressrosa</a> and resulting new bounties, she wore a collared shirt with short, ruffled sleeves and a short dark tie hung loosely around her neck. She wore short frilly skirt with&#160;a line of crosses. She had short boots with bows on the front. She also had a large <a href="/wiki/Straw_hat" class="mw-redirect" title="Straw hat">straw hat</a> with a bow and large crown on top of it.<sup id="cite_ref-chap826_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-chap826-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Series">Main Series</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Perona_Pre_Timeskip_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200119110126" class="image"><img alt="Perona Pre Timeskip Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Perona Pre Timeskip Portrait.png" data-image-key="Perona_Pre_Timeskip_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Perona_Pre_Timeskip_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20200119110126" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">A close up of Perona's face before the timeskip.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Perona_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20240802120023" class="image"><img alt="Perona Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Perona Portrait.png" data-image-key="Perona_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Perona_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20240802120023" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">A close up of Perona's face after the timeskip.

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Hungry_Days.png/revision/latest?cb=20240505041028" class="image"><img alt="Perona Hungry Days" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="74" height="140" data-image-name="Perona Hungry Days.png" data-image-key="Perona_Hungry_Days.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Hungry_Days.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/74?cb=20240505041028" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Perona in the <a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a> advertisement campaign.</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png/revision/latest?cb=20220723215545" class="image"><img alt="Perona&#39;s Shocked Face" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona&#39;s Shocked Face.png" data-image-key="Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220723215545" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png/revision/latest?cb=20220723215545" class="image"><img alt="Perona&#39;s Shocked Face" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220723215545" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona&#39;s Shocked Face.png" data-image-key="Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/84/Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220723215545" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona%27s_Shocked_Face.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona's face fault shocked at Usopp.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Perona has a very young, childlike and immature personality; frequently acting selfishly and on her own whims.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Fleeing_Thriller_Bark_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fleeing_Thriller_Bark-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She dislikes people telling her what to do<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and disobeying her will.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, she is normally loyal to <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a><sup id="cite_ref-Defeating_Straw_Hats_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defeating_Straw_Hats-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> and apparently sees him as a father-like role model, as she was crying to rejoin him after being sent to <a href="/wiki/Kuraigana_Island" title="Kuraigana Island">Kuraigana Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> After Zoro appeared on Kuraigana as well, she tended to his wounds, displaying a willingness to befriend even those she formerly knew as a foe and demonstrating that she can be kind to others, despite her normally cruel demeanor.<sup id="cite_ref-Treating_Zoro_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Treating_Zoro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She is very fond of cute things and will only allow someone to work for her if they are cute.<sup id="cite_ref-Subordinates_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Subordinates-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Her dream is to create a kingdom where all the cute things in the world have been turned into zombie animals that obey only her.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> She dislikes Kumashi because, although he is cute in appearance, his voice is not, and thus she prefers him to just be quiet.<sup id="cite_ref-Shut_Up_Kumashi_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shut_Up_Kumashi-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Her desire for cute things gives her a slightly childish outlook on some issues.<sup id="cite_ref-Subordinates_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Subordinates-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She is somewhat playful during combat, threatening to crush Usopp's heart when she was in her ghost form, which nearly caused Usopp to die from fear, and shortly afterward merely laughing it off when revealing that she could not do so.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027182107" class="image"><img alt="Perona Screaming In Fear" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona Screaming In Fear.png" data-image-key="Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20131027182107" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027182107" class="image"><img alt="Perona Screaming In Fear" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20131027182107" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona Screaming In Fear.png" data-image-key="Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20131027182107" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_Screaming_In_Fear.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona screams in fear at being covered in cockroaches.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Perona has katsaridaphobia, a fear of cockroaches, to the point of screaming and crying when Usopp covered her with fake ones.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> She is also somewhat naive, having watched Usopp seemingly lift a 10-ton hammer without questioning whether or not his feat was genuine, and shortly afterward passing out from fear when he attacked her with it, despite not actually being harmed.<sup id="cite_ref-Defeat_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defeat-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She is very confident in her Devil Fruit powers being able to defeat anyone.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Even when confronted by the powerful and dreaded <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a>, after initially being frozen with fear, Perona quickly regained her confidence and proclaimed that she would defeat him.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> She is also quite stubborn about using them in combat, having continued to use her Negative Hollows against Usopp even after they proved useless due to his negativity because she believed that his immunity was a fluke.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the timeskip, she has become more mature, although she still carries a teddy bear around, indicating that she is still obsessed with cuteness to some degree.<sup id="cite_ref-Post-Timeskip_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Post-Timeskip-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> She displayed a grateful side, as she tearfully thanked <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a> for letting her stay on his island.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Like many others, Perona has her own <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">unique laugh</a>, which uses the word Horo (e.g., "Horo-horo-horo-horo-horo!"); this is based on the name of her Devil Fruit, the <a href="/wiki/Horo_Horo_no_Mi" title="Horo Horo no Mi">Horo Horo no Mi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Perona followed her master, <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>, for at least ten years.<sup id="cite_ref-Recruiting_Hogback_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Recruiting_Hogback-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Her loyalty to him is somewhat complex: when she sensed defeat, she attempted to leave and abandon him<sup id="cite_ref-Fleeing_Thriller_Bark_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fleeing_Thriller_Bark-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> while noting that she had only stayed with him for fun,<sup id="cite_ref-For_Fun_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-For_Fun-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> but tried to take <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> down as a final gift for Moria.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Despite not clearly showing it, she is said to love Moria like a father since he found her and raised her as a child, and when the <a href="/wiki/Newspaper" title="Newspaper">newspaper</a> falsely reported that Moria died in the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Whitebeard War</a>, Perona was deeply saddened.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SBSChild_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SBSChild-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> When she learned that Moria is alive two years later, Perona is overjoyed, and she quickly departed Mihawk's castle to go find him.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Perona had a mixed relationship with her teddy bear servant, <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a>. While she considered him to be cute in appearance, she forbade him from speaking because his voice is not cute.<sup id="cite_ref-Shut_Up_Kumashi_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shut_Up_Kumashi-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> However, she was devastated when Usopp purified Kumashi.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20241117020659" class="image"><img alt="Perona Scolds Zoro" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona Scolds Zoro.png" data-image-key="Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241117020659" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20241117020659" class="image"><img alt="Perona Scolds Zoro" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241117020659" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona Scolds Zoro.png" data-image-key="Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/72/Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20241117020659" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_Scolds_Zoro.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona scolds Zoro.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While on <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, Perona became enemies with one particular member of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, due to the latter becoming the first person to ever resist the effects of her Negative Hollows<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> and later defeating her in a humiliating manner.<sup id="cite_ref-Defeat_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defeat-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> However, she also cannot help but pity Usopp who lives his life in negativity and attempts to cheer him up, though this may be for her own benefit, as she cannot make him negative unless he was already slightly positive.<sup id="cite_ref-cheerup_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cheerup-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cheerup2_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cheerup2-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> She looked down on <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> when the latter confronted her later, claiming that she could easily defeat Nami with her Mini Hollows because Usopp was her only natural enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After encountering Zoro on <a href="/wiki/Kuraigana_Island" title="Kuraigana Island">Kuraigana Island</a>, she was shocked to see him but decided to treat his wounds as he was the only other person there at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-Treating_Zoro_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Treating_Zoro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Despite their initial quarrels,<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> the two developed a relationship of mutual trust by living on the island for two years alongside <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> She also willingly brought Zoro back to <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a><sup id="cite_ref-Transporting_Zoro_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Transporting_Zoro-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and later held back the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> in order to allow the Straw Hats to escape.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dracule_Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After being sent to <a href="/wiki/Kuraigana_Island" title="Kuraigana Island">Kuraigana Island</a> by <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Kuma</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">abilities</a>, Perona decided to take residence in the castle where the at the time <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a> Mihawk lived.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Mihawk seemingly agreed or simply did not mind letting her stay with him, though he did not display any hospitality toward her beyond that.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It was shown in <a href="/wiki/From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500,000,000_Man_Arc" title="From the Decks of the World: The 500,000,000 Man Arc">From the Decks of the World: The 500,000,000 Man Arc</a> that even after going back to <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a> to retrieve <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a>, she returned to Kuraigana Island and was seen helping him with his work in tilling the land, suggesting a good status between them.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> When she learned of her old master's survival, she was upset that Mihawk did not tell her and nearly left as he told her to be safe while she tearfully thanked him for letting her stay with him.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Being formerly one of the Mysterious Four, Perona had a number of zombies under her command prior to her defection from Thriller Bark.<sup id="cite_ref-Perona_Intro_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Perona_Intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Her ex-crewmate, Doctor <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a>, acknowledges her value under Moria's employment.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Perona is physically strong, as she was seen carrying Kumashi's body, which is bigger than she is, while levitating with her Devil Fruit powers.
</p><p>Perona is able to cook, having cooked several times during the two years while she was living with Mihawk.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Medical_Knowledge">Medical Knowledge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>While she seems to recognize that bandages can help a person who is wounded, she seems to lack expertise in medicine. During the process of treating Zoro's wounds, she covered him from head to toe in an overabundance of bandages the first time she found him.<sup id="cite_ref-Treating_Zoro_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Treating_Zoro-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> However, despite this fault, she has common sense or enough knowledge of medical skills, as Zoro recovered from his injuries.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Navigation_Knowledge">Navigation Knowledge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>She is a capable navigator, demonstrated when she brought Zoro to Sabaody Archipelago all the way from Kuraigana Island.<sup id="cite_ref-Transporting_Zoro_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Transporting_Zoro-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> She later traveled to Thriller Bark and returned back to Kuraigana Island all by herself. After learning Moria was alive, she traveled to all the way to <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a> from Kuraigana Island, going from <a href="/wiki/Paradise" title="Paradise">Paradise</a> to the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Horo_Horo_no_Mi" title="Horo Horo no Mi">Horo Horo no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png/revision/latest?cb=20230902220419" class="image"><img alt="Horo Horo no Mi Power" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Horo Horo no Mi Power.png" data-image-key="Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230902220419" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png/revision/latest?cb=20230902220419" class="image"><img alt="Horo Horo no Mi Power" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230902220419" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Horo Horo no Mi Power.png" data-image-key="Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230902220419" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Horo_Horo_no_Mi_Power.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona's negative ghosts mocking her enemies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Perona ate the <a href="/wiki/Horo_Horo_no_Mi" title="Horo Horo no Mi">Horo Horo no Mi</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows her to create and control ghosts. The ghosts have the power to drain the morale, self-esteem, and will to live of anyone whom they pass through, described as hollowing out the victim's spirit.<sup id="cite_ref-Reveal_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Reveal-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> She can also create smaller ghosts that explode with enough force to damage stone walls<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> and larger ghosts that produce an even more powerful blast.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Her ghosts can also be used to form a "Ghost Network" for surveillance. This allows her to spy on enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Surveillance_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Surveillance-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> The ghosts can also duplicate themselves into even more ghosts.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to creating ghosts, she can make her own ghost leave her body. Her disembodied ghost is completely intangible; she can pass through solid objects and cannot be hit by enemy attacks, although she cannot damage anything or attack her opponents physically.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Her ghost also has the power to levitate and can change the size of her spectral body.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> However, while she is doing this, her true body remains unconscious and vulnerable.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When she was a child, Perona owned a pet bear named <a href="/wiki/Kumae" title="Kumae">Kumae</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Child_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Child-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> At some point in her childhood, she met the pirate <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a> who took her in and raised her and she eventually saw him as a father figure.<sup id="cite_ref-SBSChild_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SBSChild-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724013007" class="image"><img alt="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona.png" data-image-key="Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724013007" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724013007" class="image"><img alt="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724013007" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hogback Meets Moria, Absalom and Perona.png" data-image-key="Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f3/Hogback_Meets_Moria%2C_Absalom_and_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220724013007" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hogback_Meets_Moria,_Absalom_and_Perona.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona witnesses the meeting between Moria and Hogback.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Over 10 years ago, she joined Moria's crew merely for fun.<sup id="cite_ref-For_Fun_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-For_Fun-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> She and <a href="/wiki/Absalom" title="Absalom">Absalom</a> were present when Moria met and recruited the genius doctor, <a href="/wiki/Hogback" title="Hogback">Hogback</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Recruiting_Hogback_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Recruiting_Hogback-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Five years ago, she was sleeping while <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> was causing trouble in <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, which would later cause her to not know what he looked like when he returned.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a> tried to wake her up, she simply told him to shut up and went back to sleep.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Three and a half years ago, Perona came to Moria with news that <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> was elected the new <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, Moria brushed it off finding his moniker funny but Perona told him that he must be a strong figure to be chosen as a Warlord.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Saga">Thriller Bark Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Perona used her Ghost Network to scout out the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a><sup id="cite_ref-Ghost_Intro_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ghost_Intro-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> and later reported <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">the crew</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounties</a> to Hogback and Absalom.<sup id="cite_ref-Report_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Report-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the Dead Forest, a group of Negative Hollows encountered some of the Straw Hats and, after evading capture, demoralized <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> As the Night Attack began, Perona recalled her ghosts and rallied her <a href="/wiki/Wild_Zombies" class="mw-redirect" title="Wild Zombies">Wild Zombies</a> and <a href="/wiki/Surprise_Zombies" class="mw-redirect" title="Surprise Zombies">Surprise Zombies</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> When she left to oversee the looting of the Thousand Sunny, she ordered Kumashi to meet the <a href="/wiki/Risky_Brothers_(Zombies)" title="Risky Brothers (Zombies)">Risky Brothers</a>, who were carrying <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a> in coffins, and take them to the Dance Hall.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the Thousand Sunny, Perona was frustrated at the lack of treasure and had the food taken from the ship. <a href="/wiki/Hildon" title="Hildon">Hildon</a> reported to Perona that Moria was gathering the other members of the Mysterious Four because he had captured Luffy and would be debuting <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Zombie 900</a>, much to her surprise. Soon afterward, Perona returned to her room, where she found Absalom speaking with Kumashi about the escape of Nami, Usopp, and Chopper. After scolding Kumashi for trying to speak, Perona informed Absalom that Moria was calling them together and explained why he was doing so.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> In the Mast Mansion, the Mysterious Four discussed Luffy and the Straw Hats, and Perona reported that Nami, Usopp, and Chopper had escaped before yelling at Kumashi when he tried to correct her. When Luffy broke free from his cage, Perona quickly stopped him with her Negative Hollow before watching on as Moria removed Luffy's shadow.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> After hearing Nami, Usopp, and Chopper talking inside Kumashi and believing that it was Kumashi himself doing so, Perona proclaimed that her dream of creating a kingdom full of cute subordinates was closer to fruition with Luffy's shadow extracted. When two Spider Mice appeared and reported that <a href="/wiki/Tararan" title="Tararan">Tararan</a>'s shadow had been extracted, Hogback noted that it could only have been the "Humming Swordsman", a name which Perona did not recognize. Soon afterward, Perona accompanied the rest of the Mysterious Four to the enormous freezer containing the corpse of <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Perona watched as Moria used Luffy's shadow to revive Oars's corpse. When Oars awoke, Nami, Usopp, and Chopper screamed and fell from Kumashi's back, prompting Perona to yell at Kumashi for hiding the pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Perona continued to chastise Kumashi for hiding the pirates without letting him respond.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After reporting Oars's current activities to Moria, Perona learned that the Straw Hats had learned of the zombies' weakness to salt and were approaching them, with the General Zombies preoccupied with attending Absalom's wedding, but dismissed Hogback's worry over the zombies' weakness being known and retired to her room before attacking the Straw Hats with her ghosts, planning to weaken them enough to be taken by <a href="/wiki/Zombie#Soldier_Zombies" title="Zombie">Soldier Zombies</a>. However, Perona's attack was interrupted by Oars crashing down through the mansion.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> After Franky rebuilt the destroyed bridge, he, Zoro, Sanji, and Usopp charged into Perona's room, where Perona confronted them. After explaining the powers granted by her Devil Fruit, Perona sent a Negative Hollow through each of the Straw Hats, but Usopp was unaffected and purified several of her zombies before declaring that he was always negative, shocking Perona, who tried to cheer him up alongside her zombies before preparing to battle him.<sup id="cite_ref-cheerup_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cheerup-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Perona_vs._Usopp.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003041620" class="image"><img alt="Perona vs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona vs. Usopp.png" data-image-key="Perona_vs._Usopp.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Perona_vs._Usopp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221003041620" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Perona_vs._Usopp.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003041620" class="image"><img alt="Perona vs" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Perona_vs._Usopp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221003041620" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona vs. Usopp.png" data-image-key="Perona_vs._Usopp.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bf/Perona_vs._Usopp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221003041620" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_vs._Usopp.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona vs. Usopp.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Believing Usopp's immunity to have been a fluke, Perona sent four Negative Hollows through him, but instead became depressed herself alongside her ghosts, to the shock of her zombies.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> Soon afterward, Perona fled from Usopp while noting that she could defeat the other Straw Hats if it were not for him. After Kumashi distracted Usopp by attacking him, Perona projected her spirit from her body after hiding and tricked Usopp into believing she was flying while proclaiming that she had come up with a plan to defeat him.<sup id="cite_ref-cheerup2_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cheerup2-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Declaring that she had simply been caught up in the moment before, Perona attempted to cheer Usopp up once more before appearing behind him in a giant form. After dodging Usopp's Ageha Ryusei, Perona reverted to her normal size before placing her hands inside of Usopp's chest and pretending that she was going to crush his heart, only to reveal that she could not do such a thing. Usopp attacked her with Rokuren Mamushi Boshi, but Perona demonstrated her intangibility by letting the attack go through her and moving through the floor. When Usopp pointed out that she could not touch him either and demanded to know how she could attack him, Perona summoned some Mini Hollows and demonstrated their explosive power on a nearby wall before attacking Usopp with one as well. After tricking Usopp into running into a pillar, Perona covered his body with Mini Hollows and detonated all of them before gleefully watching Kumashi brutalize Usopp. However, Perona was shocked to see Usopp, who had donned his Sogeking mask, purify Kumashi with a salt ball before fleeing once more. Wounding Usopp with a barrage of Mini Hollow blasts once more, Perona decided to hand him over to Moria, but was surprised when Usopp figured out her trick and used Atlas Suisei to expose the room containing her true body.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206170504" class="image"><img alt="Usopp Defeats Perona" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Usopp Defeats Perona.png" data-image-key="Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20141206170504" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206170504" class="image"><img alt="Usopp Defeats Perona" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20141206170504" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Usopp Defeats Perona.png" data-image-key="Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20141206170504" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Usopp_Defeats_Perona.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Usopp defeats Perona.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Usopp deduced how she left her body by becoming a ghost in order to fight him, Perona revealed that she was a fully conscious Hollow instead of merely being a ghost controlled by her body, prompting Usopp to seemingly attack her body in an attempt to destroy it. After the attack apparently missed, a panicked Perona engulfed his body with a Toku Hollow before returning to her own body. Perona detonated the Toku Hollow but was surprised to see the explosion had disappeared as Usopp revealed he had absorbed it with an <a href="/wiki/Dials#Impact_Dial" title="Dials">Impact Dial</a>. After learning that Usopp had actually shot a Torimochi Boshi at her bed in order to trap her body in one place, Perona witnessed Usopp defeat <a href="/wiki/Hippo_Gentleman" title="Hippo Gentleman">Hippo Gentleman</a> with a blast from his Impact Dial before covering Perona herself in fake cockroaches with Kurobikari Boshi. Crying and screaming hysterically at the sight of cockroaches, a shocked Perona saw Usopp seemingly lifting a 10-ton hammer and begged him to spare her before passing out in fright as the fake hammer burst apart on impact with her. Usopp celebrated his victory over her as Perona collapsed while foaming at the mouth.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Perona's zombies found Perona still unconscious but mostly unharmed as Oars rampaged through Thriller Bark.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> Soon afterward, Perona regained consciousness and had to be calmed down by her zombies when she acted like Usopp was still attacking her. Upon seeing the damage done to the mansion by Oars, Perona wondered if the Straw Hats had done this and was shocked to learn that Oars had completely wiped out the General Zombies as well, which caused her to question if they could control him at all. However, the zombies' explanation of what was happening was interrupted by Oars punching them through one of the nearby walls while searching for Nami; witnessing this, Perona was convinced that Oars and the Straw Hats were going to completely destroy Thriller Bark and ordered her remaining subordinates to gather all the treasure and some supplies so they could leave on the Thousand Sunny.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003042609" class="image"><img alt="Perona Encounters Kuma" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="347" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona Encounters Kuma.png" data-image-key="Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221003042609" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20221003042609" class="image"><img alt="Perona Encounters Kuma" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221003042609" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="347" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona Encounters Kuma.png" data-image-key="Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e9/Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221003042609" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_Encounters_Kuma.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona meets Kuma.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Observing the battle between the Straw Hats and Oars from the Thousand Sunny, Perona admitted that she only joined Moria for fun and would not stay with him if her life were in danger before telling her subordinates that they would be leaving without delay.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> When Nami confronted her over her taking the treasure and the Thousand Sunny, Perona declared that she was planning to leave Thriller Bark on the Thousand Sunny and prepared to battle while proclaiming that her Mini Hollows should be enough to defeat Nami. However, she was interrupted by the appearance of <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a>, whom Perona was terrified at the sight of due to knowing his reputation as a cruel pirate and a Warlord of the Sea. When Kuma asked her where she would like to go on a trip, Perona described a dark, damp island with an old castle filled with malice before realizing that she had gotten caught up in his pace. Resolving to take down Kuma as a parting gift for Moria due to his shadow likely being strong, Perona prepared to attack him with a combination of Negative Hollows and a Toku Hollow, but Kuma suddenly <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">made her disappear</a> before her attack could connect, to the confusion of those watching.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Hogback and Absalom escaped Thriller Bark later, they left without Perona while noting they could not find her anywhere.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Amazon_Lily_Arc">Amazon Lily Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Perona_Finds_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20230828233755" class="image"><img alt="Perona Finds Zoro" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona Finds Zoro.png" data-image-key="Perona_Finds_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Perona_Finds_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230828233755" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Perona_Finds_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20230828233755" class="image"><img alt="Perona Finds Zoro" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Perona_Finds_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230828233755" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona Finds Zoro.png" data-image-key="Perona_Finds_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Perona_Finds_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230828233755" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_Finds_Zoro.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona encounters Zoro.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma honored Perona's request, having sent her to <a href="/wiki/Kuraigana_Island" title="Kuraigana Island">Kuraigana Island</a>, an island filled with dark and spooky ruins, in addition to the malicious castle. Although she had taken up residence in the castle, Perona was not happy because she had no servants or cute animals. As she lamented her situation while wishing she was back on Thriller Bark, Perona noticed a disturbance in the forest and discovered that Zoro had been sent to the island as well. Initially terrified by the sight of one of the Straw Hats, Perona eventually decided to save him since he was the only other person there at the time and brought him to the castle, where she treated his wounds by heavily bandaging him.
