When Zoro regained consciousness, he found out that she had taken his swords away to prevent him from attacking her.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Straw_Hat.27s_Separation_Serial"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat's_Separation_Serial">Straw Hat's Separation Serial</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Eventually, Perona returned Zoro's swords and followed him through the ruins of the island, indicating that they had developed some level of trust by then.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post_War_Arc">Post War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Mihawk_at_Home.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828093003" class="image"><img alt="Mihawk at Home" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mihawk at Home.png" data-image-key="Mihawk_at_Home.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Mihawk_at_Home.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220828093003" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Mihawk_at_Home.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828093003" class="image"><img alt="Mihawk at Home" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Mihawk_at_Home.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220828093003" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mihawk at Home.png" data-image-key="Mihawk_at_Home.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Mihawk_at_Home.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220828093003" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mihawk_at_Home.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona and Mihawk discuss Moria's fate.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, the owner of the castle that Perona was inhabiting, <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, returned to Kuraigana Island, and Perona began sobbing at the news of Moria's death in the newspaper. When Mihawk told her to cry elsewhere, Perona berated him for his lack of hospitality before listening with surprise as Mihawk revealed that he had actually seen Moria alive and well at the end of the war, though he could not definitively say whether or not he still lived.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, she helped an injured Zoro read the article about Luffy going to <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a> again by holding it up for him to read, though she complained about him taking a long time and her hands getting tired.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After accepting Zoro's request for training, Mihawk told Perona to tend to Zoro's wounds, prompting her to tell Mihawk to not order her around. Later, Perona asked Zoro about Luffy's message, so Zoro explained what it meant.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When Mihawk was teaching Zoro how to use <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a>, he forbade him from having any alcohol until he had mastered it, prompting Perona to laugh at him.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3D2Y">3D2Y</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>While Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a> were fighting the <a href="/wiki/World_Pirates" title="World Pirates">World Pirates</a>, Perona traveled to their location with <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, where she helped them by inducing despair into <a href="/wiki/Sebastian" title="Sebastian">Sebastian</a> with her Negative Hollows, defeating him. She blushed when Luffy thanked her for the help before she lost sight of the pair.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Island_Saga">Fish-Man Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Sabaody_Arc">Return to Sabaody Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After Zoro's two year-long training, Perona took him back to <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Transporting_Zoro_43-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Transporting_Zoro-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> As Luffy, Zoro, and Sanji made their way to the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Perona aided them by fending off the Marines with her Negative Hollows before demanding to know why they were still waiting around when they should be preparing to leave. After scolding Zoro for his ungrateful attitude and brushing off Sanji's infatuation with her, Perona informed the trio that battleships were surrounding the island. Later, she assisted in the Straw Hats Pirates' escape by holding back the second Marine platoon with her Negative Hollows.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World">From the Decks of the World</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921125138" class="image"><img alt="Perona Finds Kumashi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="236" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona Finds Kumashi.png" data-image-key="Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120921125138" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921125138" class="image"><img alt="Perona Finds Kumashi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120921125138" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="236" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona Finds Kumashi.png" data-image-key="Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20120921125138" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_Finds_Kumashi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona reunites with Kumashi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Much later, she left Sabaody Archipelago and returned to the wandering Thriller Bark, where she discovered Kumashi's lifeless body, much to her joy.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500.2C000.2C000_Man_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500,000,000_Man_Arc">From the Decks of the World: The 500,000,000 Man Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Perona later returned to Kuraigana Island. After the events at <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa" title="Dressrosa">Dressrosa</a>, Mihawk and Perona read the news of the Straw Hats' new bounties while tilling the land of Kuraigana Island with the humandrills.<sup id="cite_ref-chap826_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-chap826-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece:_Stampede">One Piece: Stampede</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Perona, along with Mihawk, is one of the attendees at the <a href="/wiki/Pirates_Festival" title="Pirates Festival">Pirates Festival</a>. Later, Perona used her Negative Hollow on <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a> and the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>From reading a newspaper, Perona learned that Moria was alive and was annoyed that Mihawk did not inform her about it sooner. She then prepared to leave to go find him but not before thanking Mihawk for letting her stay with him.<sup id="cite_ref-c925_35-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c925-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Red">One Piece Film: Red</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Perona flew over the sea with New Coo as they delivered the newspaper about the events on <a href="/wiki/Elegia" title="Elegia">Elegia</a>.
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Perona_Helps_Koby.png/revision/latest?cb=20240728023045" class="image"><img alt="Perona Helps Koby" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="171" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perona Helps Koby.png" data-image-key="Perona_Helps_Koby.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Perona_Helps_Koby.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240728023045" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Perona_Helps_Koby.png/revision/latest?cb=20240728023045" class="image"><img alt="Perona Helps Koby" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Perona_Helps_Koby.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240728023045" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="171" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perona Helps Koby.png" data-image-key="Perona_Helps_Koby.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Perona_Helps_Koby.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240728023045" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perona_Helps_Koby.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona helps Koby escape imprisonment.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sometime later, Perona headed to <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a>, during which she encountered <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a>. She offered him a chance to escape, so long as he helped her save Moria, which he agreed to.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> In the end, Perona was able to save Moria, and the two fled the island.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Perona vs. <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a></li>
<li>Perona vs. <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a></li>
<li>Perona vs. <a href="/wiki/Sebastian" title="Sebastian">Sebastian</a> (non-canon)</li>
<li>Perona vs. <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Arc_2">Thriller Bark Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the manga, when Usopp knocked her out, foam was coming out of her mouth;<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> this aspect of the scene was removed in the anime for unknown reasons.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Separation_Serial">Straw Hat Separation Serial</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Zoro_as_Kumashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208055913" class="image"><img alt="Zoro as Kumashi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zoro as Kumashi.png" data-image-key="Zoro_as_Kumashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Zoro_as_Kumashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130208055913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Zoro_as_Kumashi.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208055913" class="image"><img alt="Zoro as Kumashi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Zoro_as_Kumashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130208055913" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zoro as Kumashi.png" data-image-key="Zoro_as_Kumashi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7a/Zoro_as_Kumashi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20130208055913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zoro_as_Kumashi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona dresses Zoro up as Kumashi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime version of Zoro's cover story, Perona displays more of a lonely childlike personality, mostly due to living by herself with no servants. She even tries to force Zoro to be her servant by using her Negative Hollows to make him swear to be her servant and dresses him up as <a href="/wiki/Kumashi" title="Kumashi">Kumashi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the filler scenes on Kuraigana, although Perona was clearly in her ghost form, she had some interactions with physical objects despite supposedly being completely intangible.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the anime, after Luffy's message is revealed, Perona went outside the castle with Mihawk and Zoro, where she scolded Zoro for not holding off on his training until his wounds were healed.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Sabaody_Arc_2">Return to Sabaody Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When Perona is scolding Zoro at Sabaody, her hat bent in contact with the swordsman.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> This suggests that she was in her physical form rather than her ghost form; however, this does not occur in the manga.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, Sanji is aroused by Perona's scent which also would mean she is in her physical form.
</p><p>In the anime, Perona's interaction with Sanji is extended, where Sanji&#160;is beaten up and inflicted with depression by a Negative Hollow for freaking her out. Also, as she uses her ghosts to fend off the marines, Perona looks out to the sea and notes that she will have to find somebody else to play with, seemingly disappointed at Zoro's departure.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc_2">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Prior to freeing Koby from his imprisonment, Perona infiltrated Hachinosu's prison. There, she encounters two Blackbeard pirates. After the pirates were inflicted with depression by the Negative Hollows, Perona takes the keys to the cell and walks away.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> In the manga, one pirate is shown inflicted with depression while Perona freed Koby.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>An early concept of Perona from <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Green:_Secret_Pieces" title="One Piece Green: Secret Pieces">One Piece Green: Secret Pieces</a> reveals that she was originally going to be a silent, princess-like girl.
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Early_Moria.png/revision/latest?cb=20150404101559" class="image"><img alt="Early Moria" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="82" height="140" data-image-name="Early Moria.png" data-image-key="Early_Moria.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Early_Moria.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/82?cb=20150404101559" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Early Perona and her doll (Bottom left corner).
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the credits of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Stampede" title="One Piece: Stampede">One Piece: Stampede</a>, her name is spelled "Perhona".
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Perona features in the Portrait of Pirates series of figurines <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="http://mangafigures.wordpress.com/2011/01/23/ghost-princess-perona-excellent-model-one-piece-neo-dx-portraits-of-pirates-18-scale-pre-painted-pvc-figure/">in her pre-timeskip attire</a>.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemy_Appearances">Enemy Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Perona appears in the Zoro and Nami versions of the <a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a> commercials.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPerona%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 100px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png/revision/latest?cb=20211208064952" class="image"><img alt="Nami 4th Thriller Bark Outfit" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="304" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nami 4th Thriller Bark Outfit.png" data-image-key="Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20211208064952" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png/revision/latest?cb=20211208064952" class="image"><img alt="Nami 4th Thriller Bark Outfit" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20211208064952" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="304" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nami 4th Thriller Bark Outfit.png" data-image-key="Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20211208064952" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nami_4th_Thriller_Bark_Outfit.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Perona's personal Jolly Roger on Nami's shirt.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Perona has a personal <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a>, which consists of a grinning skull with sharp teeth, wearing a crown resembling Perona's own. The skull has flames on the sides of its head, another pattern beneath it which matches the color of the flames, and a cross next to either side of the skull. <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> was seen wearing a top with this Jolly Roger on it, presumably having stolen it from Perona's room after disposing of the wedding dress Absalom forced her into.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Perona was ranked 33rd, 21st, 23rd, and 25th, respectively.</li>
<li>Perona's obsession with cuteness and the style of clothing she wears both appear to be inspired by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lolita_fashion" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lolita fashion">Lolita subculture</a>.</li>
<li>Perona's favorite foods are bagel sandwiches and hot chocolate.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
